<Response>None< /Response>< review>
Love this dental office!  First off, I have the best hygienist I've ever had, I love you Kendra!!  I was never the type to enjoy going to the Dentist, even just for cleanings.   I hate the picking and the scraping, but Kendra makes me as comfortable as possible and is awesome to talk to throughout the process.  I have one tooth in particular, with a receding gum (caused by clenching at night) that is super sensitive and she always makes sure to numb it (topically) and is extra gentle while cleaning it.  It really makes all the difference, because I no longer dread my cleanings.

Then there is Dr. Jared.  He is seriously the friendliest Dentist I've ever met.  I can't say I'll ever understand it, but I am sure glad he loves teeth and smiles as much as he does!  He has a true passion not only for improving your smile and dental health, but also a genuine concern and passion for his patients.  Last year, he did some major work on one of my teeth...a really awkward shaped partial crown, which he had to make twice before he got it perfect (I think he's a bit of a perfectionist!) I was still having pain a few days afterwards and was concerned about it possibly being infected or something. He not only squeezed me in that day to check on everything, he also gave me his personal cell phone number in case it didn't improve over the weekend .  By the way, the work was perfect and there was no infection, just needed a few extra days for the nerves to heal. It feels good to know he and the ladies are always willing to take/make extra time for you when necessary, and I've never felt rushed during any of my appointments.  No matter how many questions you have or how many times he has to come back in and out of the room, he will make the time for you.   And somehow, they always manage to run on time for appointments...can't beat that!

In addition, the office staff has offered for me to bring my toddler in with me during my cleanings so that she can watch and get comfortable with the what goes on at the Dentist's office since she will soon be a patient of his as well.  I'm also going to be having our second baby come fall, which happens to be right at the time my next cleaning is due.  Since I will be a nursing Mom, I was concerned about whether or not I could bring the baby with me during my appointment.  Luckily the office is super family friendly and accommodating.  I know all the ladies will be willing to hold the baby if need be, and I'm happy to say I would be perfectly comfortable with that, because everyone there is great! HIGHLY RECOMMEND! Especially if you have a fear of Dentist's like I do....scratch that, DID.< /review>

< Review>
Fun local brewery with nice selection of brews on tap.   They will give you a sample if you can't decide.  Big seating area with a couple of outside tables.  Staff is friendly and knowledgeable about their beers and can answer questions or make suggestions if you have a style you are looking for.

No food, but lampost pizza next door will deliver to your table at superowl.  Pretty cool.</Review>

< Text>
Kudos to Bees! The fixtures were delivered to my door within 3 days, well packed and no problems!

The lights are quite a bit brighter than my old 65 watt incandescent lights and only a bit brighter than the 10 year old LED bulbs they replaced. These are 800 lumen 2700K lamps. The hue is just right for our cream colored and light green colored walls.

Most of our lamps were on 20 year old switched- analog Lutron dimmers and seemed to work well. The dimmers range between 20% and 100% brightness.

I'm grateful for the cleaner and  more modern looking fixtures. My wife very much likes them because the old baffles and trim rings looked dated (by her way of thinking). The old maxim 'Happy Wife Happy Life' applies</Text>

<review>I'm now on keto, I live in Tracy and it looks like I'll be making frequent trips to Betty's in the near future. Earlier today I told my wife that I was craving Kabobs and I really wanted to feast but didn't want to spend a bunch of money at a sit down nor did I want to fire up the grill and go through that hassle of making kabobs. A couple weeks back we passed Betty's after church but I was in a rush to get home but the smell of the Kabobs were stuck in my head since then. I called them up today and a lovely lady picked up the phone and I ordered 2 koobideh dinner plates, a skewer of tomatos, 5 skewers of koobideh and 1 skewer of chicken breasts. Let me tell you they like to add roasted jalapenos on the side for free which was an awesome bonus. All of this for less than $60!!!!! I gave them $60 and an extra $10 as tip. This much food would be well over $100 anywhere else. The owners were extremely hospitable and accommodating. I told them I would be cutting it close to their closing time and they said no worries and they waited for me. I don't think I'll ever make Kabobs at home anymore.
